\"pkg/services/apiserver/auth/authorizer/role.go\", \"symbol\": \"Authorize\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"Grafana's three-tier permission model (Viewer/Editor/Admin) is implemented across several layers:\\n\\n## 1. Role Type Definition\\n\\n**`pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go`** is the foundational file. It defines `RoleType` as a string, the four constants (`RoleNone`, `RoleViewer`, `RoleEditor`, `RoleAdmin`), and the `rolePrecedence` map that establishes the hierarchy (None=10, Viewer=20, Editor=30, Admin=40). The key `Includes(other RoleType) bool` method uses this precedence map to check if a role encompasses a lower role (e.g., Admin includes Editor and Viewer). `Parents()` and `Children()` methods also traverse the hierarchy.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/org/model.go`** re-exports `RoleType` and the role constants from the identity package, and defines `OrgUser` (the DB model linking a user to an org with a `RoleType` role).\\n\\n## 2. Role-to-Permission Mapping\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go`** defines:\\n- Constants like `BasicRolePrefix`, `FixedRolePrefix`, `RoleGrafanaAdmin`, `FixedCloudViewerRole/EditorRole/AdminRole`\\n- `BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()`: builds the basic role DTOs (basic:viewer, basic:editor, basic:admin, basic:none, basic:grafana_admin) keyed by org role string\\n- `DeclareFixedRoles(service, cfg)`: declares all OSS fixed roles and their grants to the three org roles\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go`** and **`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go`** declare the `fixed:folders:viewer/editor/admin` and `fixed:dashboards:viewer/editor/admin` roles, mapping them to permission action sets and granting them to the corresponding basic org roles.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/service.go`** implements the core access control service including `DeclareFixedRoles`, `GetUserPermissions`, `getBasicRolePermissions`, and `getCachedBasicRolesPermissions`—the logic that resolves what permissions a user has based on their basic role (Viewer/Editor/Admin).\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/database/database.go`** provides the store layer: `GetUsersBasicRoles` returns a map of userID→[]string of role names (Admin, Editor, Viewer, Grafana Admin), and `GetBasicRolesPermissions` fetches all permissions assigned to the user's basic roles via the `builtin_role` table.\\n\\n## 3. Permission Guard Middleware\\n\\n**`pkg/middleware/middleware.go`** defines the pre-built middleware guards:\\n- `ReqGrafanaAdmin` — requires Grafana server admin\\n- `ReqEditorRole = RoleAuth(org.RoleEditor, org.RoleAdmin)` — allows Editor or Admin org role\\n- `ReqOrgAdmin = RoleAuth(org.RoleAdmin)` — allows only Admin org role\\n\\n**`pkg/middleware/auth.go`** implements:\\n- `RoleAuth(roles ...org.RoleType) web.Handler`: checks if `c.OrgRole` exactly matches any of the provided roles; denies if not\\n- `Auth(options *AuthOptions) web.Handler`: checks sign-in status and Grafana admin flag\\n- `CanAdminPlugins`, `RoleAppPluginAuth`: additional guards using RBAC evaluators\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go`** implements the RBAC-based middleware:\\n- `Middleware(ac AccessControl) func(Evaluator) web.Handler`: wraps an RBAC `Evaluator` (e.g., `EvalPermission(\\\"dashboards:read\\\", scope)`) into a web handler that calls `ac.Evaluate()` against the signed-in user\\n- `authorize(c, ac, user, evaluator)`: injects URL params into scope templates and evaluates access\\n- `AuthorizeInOrgMiddleware`: resolves user identity in a target org before evaluating permissions\\n\\n**`pkg/services/apiserver/auth/authorizer/role.go`** implements the Kubernetes API server authorizer using org roles: Admin gets full access, Editor gets get/list/watch/create/update/patch/delete/put/post, and Viewer/None get only get/list/watch.\\n\\n**`pkg/api/accesscontrol.go`** declares all HTTP server fixed roles and their grants to org roles via `declareFixedRoles()`.\\n\\n## 4. Folder/Dashboard Permission Inheritance\\n\\n**`pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go`** is the central file for permission inheritance:\\n- Defines all action and scope constants (`ActionFoldersRead`, `ActionDashboardsWrite`, `ScopeFoldersPrefix`, etc.)\\n- `GetInheritedScopes(ctx, orgID, folderUID, folderSvc)`: walks up the folder tree via `folderSvc.GetParents()` and returns The Includes(other RoleType) bool method uses this precedence map to check if a role encompasses a lower role. Parents() and Children() methods traverse the hierarchy.\\n\\npkg/services/org/model.go re-exports RoleType and the role constants from the identity package, and defines OrgUser (the DB model linking a user to an org with a RoleType role).\\n\\n2.
